### Post by flyrs45 on 2013-08-25
Ok first off I apologize cause I know that a few threads have already been posted on this but they dont see too clear and havent been much help. Ok first off let me tell you I am brand new to linux and not the most computer savy in general although I would say I am not completly stupid. I have an old Dell Inspiron 15 that had a couple viruses and I ended up getting a new laptop eventually and therefore this dell was gathering dust and was no use. I would like to have a laptop just to mess around with programming and decided to install ubuntu on this old laptop. I installed ubuntu but couldnt get the wifi card to work and couldnt and tried a few things to no avail. So I decided ( probably a dumb idea) to re-install Ubuntu and i ended up getting the error in the title. I ran the smart scan and everything seems fine

### Post by Quackers on 2013-08-25
I would hazard a guess that the hard drive is failing. I understand that the smart status lists it as ok but something set this message off.
If you go to the hard drive's manufacturer (not the laptop's) they will have a test utility for their hard drives. You could run that and see if bad sectors are found.

Alternatively you could try re-installing with the partitions changed and see if the same thing happens.

---

Its 

the ext4 file system creation in partition #1 of SCSI3 (0,0,0) (sda) failed

idk if that changes anything... And should I run badblocks

---

### Post by Quackers on 2013-08-25
Oh, it seems that the file system creation failed. That's different, it's a partitioning problem in the installer.  I used to get something similar on an older computer and it eventually ran ok, so I never actually found the cause. I would just keep trying to install and hopefully it will work.
